2010-05-06 17:58:07 +0200 (Thu, 06 May 2010), revision 3164, ekolin
The build system creates manifest files using UTF-8 character
encoding, but ant assumes by default that a manifest file uses the
local platform encoding, thus we must tell ant that the generated
manifest file use UTF-8 when adding it to a bundle jar.
U   knopflerfish.org/branches/kf3/ant/bundlebuild.xml

Added new ant property, root.out.dir, that may be used to controll where all intermidiate build products are placed. The top-level distrib-target now uses this to avoid sharing intermidiate build results with in source builds.
